So GT contains **all** of these structural elements:

- a \(v^3\) term (odd power, sign-preserving),

Any candidate must be able to represent **simultaneously**: \(\sin(t)\), \(v^3\), \(v\), and \(x + x t\). Candidates may include extra terms only if they can be zeroed out by parameter choices.

Let me check each candidate systematically. The key requirements are: `v**3`, `v`, `x*t`, `x`, and `sin(t)`.

- Most candidates lack `sin(t)` and `x*t` terms

None of the candidates have both `sin(t)` and `x*t` as required basis functions. The GT requires these linearly independent functions, and since polynomials, exponentials, trigonometric functions, and square roots are all linearly independent, no candidate can reproduce the GT.
